< Text>
Not really able to tell what the service or atmosphere is like normally due to the social distancing protocols not allowing seating yet, however the food was delicious! We ordered the cheese tortellini, fried ravioli, and cheese garlic bread. Each one had flavorful and ample amounts of cheese, and nothing tasted like it was simply reheated in the microwave (I'm looking at you, Olive Garden). The selection on the menu was fairly typical of most Italian restaurants, with a few added items like hamburgers and tacos (what place doesn't sell tacos in LA?) and the wine menu was a little lacking, but as someone who doesn't really care if they have the most fancy Bordeaux on hand, it was a fine selection. Overall, I will say that this is one of my new favorites for Italian food, and will definitely be returning. Salud!<//Text>

First time I visited this place it was about 10 years ago. There's been minor changes to it but this one of the best small Italian restaurants I've been to, if not best one ever. There hasn't been a single time when food wasn't exceptional, either the pasta or the pizza. Draft beer also available. <Rate>4</Rate>< Text>
Despite its humble facade, Panini Pizzeria is solid spot for Italian cuisine on the world famous Sunset Strip. Whether it's table service or takeout you want, this place does it all and does it well.
In my experience you can never go wrong with a pizza, my personal favourite bring the BBQ Chicken. I will also never say no to their Mozzarella sticks! Service is always friendly and fast and it's fun to sit on the patio and people watch when you have the chance. Popular with locals and tourists alike, Panini is definitely worth a visit.< /Text>

< Text>
Train Horns. Do not live here if you are a light sleeper or cannot stand loud noise. I had moved here from the east coast a year ago, and wish I had read some of the reviews here beforehand.

The complex is located near 3 street crossings (65th, 66th, & 67th St), which trains are required by law to use their horn for each crossing at least once. This often lasts in 30 second intervals, at more than 20+ times a day. I typically would hear at least 3-5 trains every night between 9pm - 3am, which I was not able to sleep through for year.

If you are working from home during COVID, the train vibrations/horns will definitely interfere with meetings/calls. Spend some time at Public Market for a few hours to see if the location is the right fit for you.< /Text>

< Text>
I was relocating from New York and had been visiting apartments since the moment I stepped off the plane on Saturday morning. It was a frustrating couple of hours, as none of the apartments had the total package I was looking for. Artistry wasn't on my schedule for apartments to see, but I happened to pass it during my drive through Emeryville. Erica B was the leasing team member I was lucky to be paired with.

She made the experience very personal from the very beginning. She is similar in age and had similar interests, so we established rapport pretty quickly. She answered all of my questions very honestly, preparing me for what to expect throughout my stay. She even gave me tips on the type of cooling system I should get to keep my apartment at a comfortable temperature level.

I was originally looking for a 1br/1bath, with a pool being a must have amenity, however, because of the experience she created for me, I settled for a studio at Artistry. Artistry doesn't have a pool, but it does have a hot tub and a grilling area/court yard. Everything about it felt right instantly, which was definitely enough for me to be more flexible about what I was looking for.

Is there train noise? Yeah. Am I ok with it? Yeah.
Is there sometimes noise in the halls from other residents walking in or out? Yeah. I am also ok with it. I also see some comments about not getting all of the deposit back. The deposit for studios and 1 bedrooms are only $400... thats not much compared to most places in New York and some of the other places I visited in the Bay Area. Most of that deposit ends up going towards cleaning costs. Erica was very open about everything I should expect when I visited the apartment. Had she not told me, I would probably be much more irritated. She has been extremely transparent and helpful since I moved in on Tuesday and I feel extra comfortable knowing I can shoot her an email and get helped right away.

I have needed maintenance during the short time I've been here, for small things, such as, some tightening on some of the things in the apartment and help using the service elevator for furniture deliveries. Erica helped set that up immediately. Jorge came and fixed one of the cabinets in the bathroom. She asked also Jorge to meet my delivery guys the other morning. Jorge is also great! Super friendly and very helpful.

I'm a little unsure when I read the reviews below, as this has not been my experience with Artistry at all. It was exceptional.

Thanks again for the great service!<//Text>

<Review>The food here is not all that great but it is not bad. Plus in most cases, I am not a fan of, to begin with. But once in a while, I feel like having something different. This is when I go to Arbys. Having a place in a smaller town like this is excellent. It is because it is something different than most of all those other fast food places.

The staff here is , and the place looks immaculate.
This is always a plus!

The lines are usually not to bad either.

All in all, this is a great place to go if you want something different from the familiar, usually fast food places that you might go to.

I do enjoy the Gyros. Many times you can get them two for six dollars that is a good deal.

Moreover, oh, They have lovely delicious french fries!
They are the best!

They also have rootbeer floats if you are into that kind of stuff. Personally I am not, but I know many are. Most places do not have that as an option. Also, Don't forget their mozzarella cheese sticks those are exceedingly delicious as well.<//Review>< pics>
